function ListOrderCells(cells) {
	var lst = [];
	var max_x = cells.length, max_y = 0;
	for (var x = 0; x < max_x; x++) {
		for (var y = 0, max_y = cells[x].length; y < max_y; y++) {
			var cell = cells[x][y];
			if (0 != cell["order"]) {
				lst.push({ "coordinate-x": x, "coordinate-y": y, "info": cell });
			}
		}
	}
	lst.sort(function (cell_a, cell_b) {
		return cell_b["info"]["order"] - cell_a["info"]["order"];
	});
	return { "cells": lst, "max-cordinate-x": max_x };
};

function CompareCells(cells_order, maxx_order, cells_new, maxx_new, distx_new) {
	var distx_order = maxx_order - dist_new;
	cells_order.forEach(function (cell_order, index, array) {
		var cell_new = cells_new[cell_order["coordinate-x"] - dist_order][cell_order["coordinate-y"]];
		if (cell_new[""])
	});

};
